\begin{Indent}\textbf{ decode}\par
{\em Creates an array containing the numeric code points of each Unicode character in the string.

While Java\+Script uses U\+C\+S-\/2 internally, this function will convert a pair of surrogate halves (each of which U\+C\+S-\/2 exposes as separate characters) into a single code point, matching U\+T\+F-\/16. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
{\ttfamily punycode.\+ucs2.\+encode} 

\href{https://mathiasbynens.be/notes/javascript-encoding}{\texttt{ https\+://mathiasbynens.\+be/notes/javascript-\/encoding}} @member\+Of punycode.\+ucs2
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em \{\+String\}} & string The Unicode input string (U\+C\+S-\/2). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\{Array\} The new array of code points. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsection*{encode}
\label{_amgrp97a57645a3f0e1518f8c9f4d340d4c4f}%
Creates a string based on an array of numeric code points.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
{\ttfamily punycode.\+ucs2.\+decode} @member\+Of punycode.\+ucs2
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em \{\+Array\}} & code\+Points The array of numeric code points. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\{String\} The new Unicode string (U\+C\+S-\/2). 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Converts a digit/integer into a basic code point. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
{\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{dist_2markdown-it_8js_a7bedb5802834afc9a1f22bc90c439c19}{basic\+To\+Digit()}}}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em \{\+Number\}} & digit The numeric value of a basic code point. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\{Number\} The basic code point whose value (when used for representing integers) is {\ttfamily digit}, which needs to be in the range {\ttfamily 0} to {\ttfamily base -\/ 1}. If {\ttfamily flag} is non-\/zero, the uppercase form is used; else, the lowercase form is used. The behavior is undefined if {\ttfamily flag} is non-\/zero and {\ttfamily digit} has no uppercase form. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{dist_2markdown-it_8js_a113d2032c3a577d56d33372bee60ca76}\label{dist_2markdown-it_8js_a113d2032c3a577d56d33372bee60ca76}} 
\index{markdown-\/it.js@{markdown-\/it.js}!LinkifyIt@{LinkifyIt}}
\index{LinkifyIt@{LinkifyIt}!markdown-\/it.js@{markdown-\/it.js}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{LinkifyIt()}{LinkifyIt()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily function Linkify\+It (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{schemas,  }\item[{}]{options }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



class Linkify\+It 

new Linkify\+It(schemas, options)
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item schemas (Object)\+: Optional. Additional schemas to validate (prefix/validator)
\item options (Object)\+: \{ fuzzy\+Link$\vert$fuzzy\+Email$\vert$fuzzy\+IP\+: true$\vert$false \}
\end{DoxyItemize}

Creates new linkifier instance with optional additional schemas. Can be called without {\ttfamily new} keyword for convenience.

By default understands\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily http(s)\+://...} , {\ttfamily \href{ftp://..}{\texttt{ ftp\+://..}}.}, {\ttfamily mailto\+:...} \& {\ttfamily //...} links
\item \char`\"{}fuzzy\char`\"{} links and emails (example.\+com, \href{mailto:foo@bar.com}{\texttt{ foo@bar.\+com}}).
\end{DoxyItemize}

{\ttfamily schemas} is an object, where each key/value describes protocol/rule\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{key}} -\/ link prefix (usually, protocol name with {\ttfamily \+:} at the end, {\ttfamily skype\+:} for example). {\ttfamily linkify-\/it} makes shure that prefix is not preceeded with alphanumeric char and symbols. Only whitespaces and punctuation allowed.
\item {\bfseries{value}} -\/ rule to check tail after link prefix
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\itshape String} -\/ just alias to existing rule
\item {\itshape Object}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\itshape validate} -\/ validator function (should return matched length on success), or {\ttfamily Reg\+Exp}.
\item {\itshape normalize} -\/ optional function to normalize text \& url of matched result (for example, for @twitter mentions).
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}

{\ttfamily options}\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{fuzzy\+Link}} -\/ recognige U\+R\+L-\/s without {\ttfamily http(s)\+:} prefix. Default {\ttfamily true}.
\item {\bfseries{fuzzy\+IP}} -\/ allow I\+Ps in fuzzy links above. Can conflict with some texts like version numbers. Default {\ttfamily false}.
\item {\bfseries{fuzzy\+Email}} -\/ recognize emails without {\ttfamily mailto\+:} prefix. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{dist_2markdown-it_8js_a1e1222231fe533c404c312d2a079ff80}\label{dist_2markdown-it_8js_a1e1222231fe533c404c312d2a079ff80}} 
\index{markdown-\/it.js@{markdown-\/it.js}!map@{map}}
\index{map@{map}!markdown-\/it.js@{markdown-\/it.js}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{map()}{map()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily function map (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{array,  }\item[{}]{fn }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{dist_2markdown-it_8js_a39a8280bbc91dffecb5bc7a7fd8681df}\label{dist_2markdown-it_8js_a39a8280bbc91dffecb5bc7a7fd8681df}} 
\index{markdown-\/it.js@{markdown-\/it.js}!MarkdownIt@{MarkdownIt}}
\index{MarkdownIt@{MarkdownIt}!markdown-\/it.js@{markdown-\/it.js}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MarkdownIt()}{MarkdownIt()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily function Markdown\+It (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{preset\+Name,  }\item[{}]{options }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



class Markdown\+It 

Main parser/renderer class.

\label{dist_2markdown-it_8js_autotoc_md1314}%
\Hypertarget{dist_2markdown-it_8js_autotoc_md1314}%
\doxysubparagraph*{Usage}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{// node.js, "classic" way:}
\DoxyCodeLine{var MarkdownIt = require('markdown-\/it'),}
\DoxyCodeLine{    md = new MarkdownIt();}
\DoxyCodeLine{var result = md.render('\# markdown-\/it rulezz!');}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{// node.js, the same, but with sugar:}
\DoxyCodeLine{var md = require('markdown-\/it')();}
\DoxyCodeLine{var result = md.render('\# markdown-\/it rulezz!');}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{// browser without AMD, added to "window" on script load}
\DoxyCodeLine{// Note, there are no dash.}
\DoxyCodeLine{var md = window.markdownit();}
\DoxyCodeLine{var result = md.render('\# markdown-\/it rulezz!');}
\end{DoxyCode}


Single line rendering, without paragraph wrap\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var md = require('markdown-\/it')();}
\DoxyCodeLine{var result = md.renderInline('\_\_markdown-\/it\_\_ rulezz!');}
\end{DoxyCode}
 new \mbox{\hyperlink{lib_2jsdoc_2util_2markdown_8js_a9bb038ec346f24c740de74494c96126b}{Markdown\+It(\mbox{[}preset\+Name, options\mbox{]})}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item preset\+Name (String)\+: optional, {\ttfamily commonmark} / {\ttfamily zero}
\item options (Object)
\end{DoxyItemize}

Creates parser instanse with given config. Can be called without {\ttfamily new}.

\label{dist_2markdown-it_8js_autotoc_md1315}%
\Hypertarget{dist_2markdown-it_8js_autotoc_md1315}%
\doxysubparagraph*{preset\+Name}

Markdown\+It provides named presets as a convenience to quickly enable/disable active syntax rules and options for common use cases.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/markdown-it/markdown-it/blob/master/lib/presets/commonmark.js}{\texttt{ \char`\"{}commonmark\char`\"{}}} -\/ configures parser to strict \href{http://commonmark.org/}{\texttt{ Common\+Mark}} mode.
\item \href{https://github.com/markdown-it/markdown-it/blob/master/lib/presets/default.js}{\texttt{ default}} -\/ similar to G\+FM, used when no preset name given. Enables all available rules, but still without html, typographer \& autolinker.
\item \href{https://github.com/markdown-it/markdown-it/blob/master/lib/presets/zero.js}{\texttt{ \char`\"{}zero\char`\"{}}} -\/ all rules disabled. Useful to quickly setup your config via {\ttfamily .\mbox{\hyperlink{dist_2markdown-it_8js_a44f74913494bbd4bd28f3ede02e96fe4}{enable()}}}. For example, when you need only {\ttfamily bold} and {\ttfamily italic} markup and nothing else.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\label{dist_2markdown-it_8js_autotoc_md1316}%
\Hypertarget{dist_2markdown-it_8js_autotoc_md1316}%
\doxysubparagraph*{options\+:}


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{html}} -\/ {\ttfamily false}. Set {\ttfamily true} to enable H\+T\+ML tags in source. Be careful! That\textquotesingle{}s not safe! You may need external sanitizer to protect output from X\+SS. It\textquotesingle{}s better to extend features via plugins, instead of enabling H\+T\+ML.
\item {\bfseries{xhtml\+Out}} -\/ {\ttfamily false}. Set {\ttfamily true} to add \textquotesingle{}/\textquotesingle{} when closing single tags ({\ttfamily $<$br /$>$}). This is needed only for full Common\+Mark compatibility. In real world you will need H\+T\+ML output.
\item {\bfseries{breaks}} -\/ {\ttfamily false}. Set {\ttfamily true} to convert {\ttfamily \textbackslash{}n} in paragraphs into {\ttfamily $<$br$>$}.
\item {\bfseries{lang\+Prefix}} -\/ {\ttfamily language-\/}. C\+SS language class prefix for fenced blocks. Can be useful for external highlighters.
\item {\bfseries{linkify}} -\/ {\ttfamily false}. Set {\ttfamily true} to autoconvert U\+R\+L-\/like text to links.
\item {\bfseries{typographer}} -\/ {\ttfamily false}. Set {\ttfamily true} to enable \href{https://github.com/markdown-it/markdown-it/blob/master/lib/rules_core/replacements.js}{\texttt{ some language-\/neutral replacement}} + quotes beautification (smartquotes).
\item {\bfseries{quotes}} -\/ {\ttfamily “”‘’}, String or Array. Double + single quotes replacement pairs, when typographer enabled and smartquotes on. For example, you can use `\textquotesingle{}«»„“'{\ttfamily for Russian,}\textquotesingle{}„“‚‘\textquotesingle{}{\ttfamily for German, and }\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}«\textbackslash{}x\+A0\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}x\+A0»\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}‹\textbackslash{}x\+A0\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}x\+A0›\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}{\ttfamily for French (including nbsp).}
\item {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+highlight\+\_\+\+\_\+ -\/}null{\ttfamily . Highlighter function for fenced code blocks. Highlighter}function (str, lang)\`{} should return escaped H\+T\+ML. It can also return empty string if the source was not changed and should be escaped externaly. If result starts with $<$pre... internal wrapper is skipped.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\label{dist_2markdown-it_8js_autotoc_md1317}%
\Hypertarget{dist_2markdown-it_8js_autotoc_md1317}%
\doxysubparagraph*{Example}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{// commonmark mode}
\DoxyCodeLine{var md = require('markdown-\/it')('commonmark');}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{// default mode}
\DoxyCodeLine{var md = require('markdown-\/it')();}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{// enable everything}
\DoxyCodeLine{var md = require('markdown-\/it')(\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  html: true,}
\DoxyCodeLine{  linkify: true,}
\DoxyCodeLine{  typographer: true}
\DoxyCodeLine{\});}
\end{DoxyCode}

\DoxyCodeLine{}

\DoxyCodeLine{\});}
\end{DoxyCode}


Or with full wrapper override (if you need assign class to \`{}
\begin{DoxyPre}`):\end{DoxyPre}



\begin{DoxyPre}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{// Actual default values}
\DoxyCodeLine{var md = require('markdown-\/it')(\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  highlight: function (str, lang) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{    if (lang \&\& hljs.getLanguage(lang)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{      try \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{        return '<pre class="hljs"><code>' +}
\DoxyCodeLine{               hljs.highlight(str, \{ language: lang, ignoreIllegals: true \}).value +}
\DoxyCodeLine{               '</code></pre>';}
\DoxyCodeLine{      \} catch (\_\_) \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{    return '<pre class="hljs"><code>' + md.utils.escapeHtml(str) + '</code></pre>';}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\});}
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyPre}
Markdown\+It\+::inline -\/$>$ Parser\+Inline

Instance of \mbox{[}\mbox{[}Parser\+Inline\mbox{]}\mbox{]}. You may need it to add new rules when writing plugins. For simple rules control use \mbox{[}\mbox{[}Markdown\+It.\+disable\mbox{]}\mbox{]} and \mbox{[}\mbox{[}Markdown\+It.\+enable\mbox{]}\mbox{]}.

Markdown\+It\+::block -\/$>$ Parser\+Block

Instance of \mbox{[}\mbox{[}Parser\+Block\mbox{]}\mbox{]}. You may need it to add new rules when writing plugins. For simple rules control use \mbox{[}\mbox{[}Markdown\+It.\+disable\mbox{]}\mbox{]} and \mbox{[}\mbox{[}Markdown\+It.\+enable\mbox{]}\mbox{]}.

Markdown\+It\+::core -\/$>$ Core

Instance of \mbox{[}\mbox{[}Core\mbox{]}\mbox{]} chain executor. You may need it to add new rules when writing plugins. For simple rules control use \mbox{[}\mbox{[}Markdown\+It.\+disable\mbox{]}\mbox{]} and \mbox{[}\mbox{[}Markdown\+It.\+enable\mbox{]}\mbox{]}.

Markdown\+It\+::renderer -\/$>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classRenderer}{Renderer}}

Instance of \mbox{[}\mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classRenderer}{Renderer}}\mbox{]}\mbox{]}. Use it to modify output look. Or to add rendering rules for new token types, generated by plugins.

\Hypertarget{markdown-it.js_autotoc_md1319}%

Markdown\+It\+::linkify -\/$>$ Linkify\+It

\href{https://github.com/markdown-it/linkify-it}{\texttt{ linkify-\/it}} instance. Used by \href{https://github.com/markdown-it/markdown-it/blob/master/lib/rules_core/linkify.js}{\texttt{ linkify}} rule.

Markdown\+It\+::validate\+Link(url) -\/$>$ Boolean

Link validation function. Common\+Mark allows too much in links. By default we disable {\ttfamily javascript\+:}, {\ttfamily vbscript\+:}, {\ttfamily file\+:} schemas, and almost all {\ttfamily data\+:...} schemas except some embedded image types.

You can change this behaviour\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var md = require('markdown-\/it')();}
\DoxyCodeLine{// enable everything}
\DoxyCodeLine{md.validateLink = function () \{ return true; \}}
\end{DoxyCode}


Markdown\+It\+::normalize\+Link(url) -\/$>$ String

Function used to encode link url to a machine-\/readable format, which includes url-\/encoding, punycode, etc.

Markdown\+It\+::normalize\+Link\+Text(url) -\/$>$ String

Function used to decode link url to a human-\/readable format\`{}

Markdown\+It\+::utils -\/$>$ utils

Assorted utility functions, useful to write plugins. See details \href{https://github.com/markdown-it/markdown-it/blob/master/lib/common/utils.js}{\texttt{ here}}.

Markdown\+It\+::helpers -\/$>$ helpers

Link components parser functions, useful to write plugins. chainable, internal Markdown\+It.\+configure(presets) 

Batch load of all options and compenent settings. This is internal method, and you probably will not need it. But if you will -\/ see available presets and data structure \href{https://github.com/markdown-it/markdown-it/tree/master/lib/presets}{\texttt{ here}}

We strongly recommend to use presets instead of direct config loads. That will give better compatibility with next versions. \mbox{\Hypertarget{dist_2markdown-it_8js_a3d49f572e26c3a10b93da74045bb4d9f}\label{dist_2markdown-it_8js_a3d49f572e26c3a10b93da74045bb4d9f}}

\index{damp@{damp}!markdown-\/it.js@{markdown-\/it.js}}

chainable Markdown\+It.\+enable(list, ignore\+Invalid) 


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item list (String$\vert$\+Array)\+: rule name or list of rule names to enable
\item ignore\+Invalid (Boolean)\+: set {\ttfamily true} to ignore errors when rule not found.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Enable list or rules. It will automatically find appropriate components, containing rules with given names. If rule not found, and {\ttfamily ignore\+Invalid} not set -\/ throws exception.

Linkify\+It\+::match(text) -\/$>$ Array$\vert$null. 

Returns array of found link descriptions or {\ttfamily null} on fail. We strongly recommend to use \mbox{[}\mbox{[}Linkify\+It\+::test\mbox{]}\mbox{]} first, for best speed.

\label{dist_2markdown-it_8js_autotoc_md1313}%
\Hypertarget{dist_2markdown-it_8js_autotoc_md1313}%
\doxysubparagraph*{\mbox{\hyperlink{classResult}{Result}} match description}


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{schema}} -\/ link schema, can be empty for fuzzy links, or {\ttfamily //} for protocol-\/neutral links.
\item {\bfseries{index}} -\/ offset of matched text
\item {\bfseries{last\+Index}} -\/ index of next char after mathch end
\item {\bfseries{raw}} -\/ matched text
\item {\bfseries{text}} -\/ normalized text
\item {\bfseries{url}} -\/ link, generated from matched text 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{dist_2markdown-it_8js_a2eafae98a5af9a0036e375c6c071d4ea}\label{dist_2markdown-it_8js_a2eafae98a5af9a0036e375c6c071d4ea}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{markdown-it_2lib_2index_8js_a39a8280bbc91dffecb5bc7a7fd8681df}{Markdown\+It}} \mbox{\hyperlink{wrapperLodash_8js_ae07a24b9237d93a82e7e0aeb67eecca0}{prototype}} parse}



internal Markdown\+It.\+parse(src, env) -\/$>$ Array 


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item src (String)\+: source string
\item env (Object)\+: environment sandbox
\end{DoxyItemize}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classParse}{Parse}} input string and return list of block tokens (special token type \char`\"{}inline\char`\"{} will contain list of inline tokens). You should not call this method directly, until you write custom renderer (for example, to produce A\+ST).

{\ttfamily env} is used to pass data between \char`\"{}distributed\char`\"{} rules and return additional metadata like reference info, needed for the renderer. It also can be used to inject data in specific cases. Usually, you will be ok to pass {\ttfamily \{\}}, and then pass updated object to renderer. \mbox{\Hypertarget{dist_2markdown-it_8js_a7af768f2807664d0426fff9a343f7797}\label{dist_2markdown-it_8js_a7af768f2807664d0426fff9a343f7797}}

{\ttfamily env} can be used to inject additional metadata ({\ttfamily \{\}} by default). But you will not need it with high probability. chainable Linkify\+It\+::set(options) 

chainable Markdown\+It.\+set(options)


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item options (Object)\+: \{ fuzzy\+Link$\vert$fuzzy\+Email$\vert$fuzzy\+IP\+: true$\vert$false \}
\end{DoxyItemize}

Set recognition options for links without schema.

Set parser options (in the same format as in constructor). Probably, you will never need it, but you can change options after constructor call.

\label{dist_2markdown-it_8js_autotoc_md1320}%
\Hypertarget{dist_2markdown-it_8js_autotoc_md1320}%
\doxysubparagraph*{Example}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var md = require('markdown-\/it')()}
\DoxyCodeLine{            .set(\{ html: true, breaks: true \})}
\DoxyCodeLine{            .set(\{ typographer, true \});}
\end{DoxyCode}


{\bfseries{Note\+:}} To achieve the best possible performance, don\textquotesingle{}t modify a {\ttfamily markdown-\/it} instance options on the fly. If you need multiple configurations it\textquotesingle{}s best to create multiple instances and initialize each with separate config. \mbox{\Hypertarget{dist_2markdown-it_8js_a9de438e19cd2de26d8dbb33be7a5832c}\label{dist_2markdown-it_8js_a9de438e19cd2de26d8dbb33be7a5832c}}

chainable Linkify\+It\+::tlds(list \mbox{[}, keep\+Old\mbox{]}) -\/$>$ this 


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item list (Array)\+: list of tlds
\item keep\+Old (Boolean)\+: merge with current list if {\ttfamily true} ({\ttfamily false} by default)
\end{DoxyItemize}

Load (or merge) new tlds list. Those are user for fuzzy links (without prefix) to avoid false positives. By default this algorythm used\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item hostname with any 2-\/letter root zones are ok.
\item biz$\vert$com$\vert$edu$\vert$gov$\vert$net$\vert$org$\vert$pro$\vert$web$\vert$xxx$\vert$aero$\vert$asia$\vert$coop$\vert$info$\vert$museum$\vert$name$\vert$shop$\vert$рф are ok.
\item encoded ({\ttfamily xn-\/-\/...}) root zones are ok.
\end{DoxyItemize}

If list is replaced, then exact match for 2-\/chars root zones will be checked. \mbox{\Hypertarget{dist_2markdown-it_8js_af35e177893b51b8859e001c4aafa51d6}\label{dist_2markdown-it_8js_af35e177893b51b8859e001c4aafa51d6}} 
\index{markdown-\/it.js@{markdown-\/it.js}!tlds\_2ch\_src\_re@{tlds\_2ch\_src\_re}}
\index{tlds\_2ch\_src\_re@{tlds\_2ch\_src\_re}!markdown-\/it.js@{markdown-\/it.js}}

chainable Markdown\+It.\+use(plugin, params) 

Load specified plugin with given params into current parser instance. It\textquotesingle{}s just a sugar to call {\ttfamily plugin(md, params)} with curring.
